{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01EnrXCNwAuBm9X94TszupUV","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01Fnq9YpaYKbEzeSvpL5TzQW","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Cilium eBPF Map API Reference\n\nThis document provides comprehensive API reference documentation for Cilium's eBPF map API in the `pkg/bpf` package. The API provides Go wrappers for user-space interaction with kernel eBPF maps.\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Core Map Type and Creation](#core-map-type-and-creation)\n2. [CRUD Operations](#crud-operations)\n3. [Iteration and Dumping](#iteration-and-dumping)\n4. [Pinning and Persistence](#pinning-and-persistence)\n5. [Key/Value Interfaces](#keyvalue-interfaces)\n6. [Event System](#event-system)\n7. [Collection Loading](#collection-loading)\n8. [Usage Examples](#usage-examples)\n\n## Core Map Type and Creation\n\n### Map Type\n\nThe `Map` type represents a BPF map and provides all operations for user-space interaction with kernel eBPF maps.\n\n```go\ntype Map struct {\n    Logger *slog.Logger\n    // ... internal fields\n}\n```\n\n### Creating Maps\n\n#### NewMap\n\nCreates a new `Map` instance with the specified configuration. The map is not yet created in the kernel.\n\n```go\nfunc NewMap(\n    name string,\n    mapType ebpf.MapType,\n    mapKey MapKey,\n    mapValue MapValue,\n    maxEntries int,\n    flags uint32,\n) *Map\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `name`: The map name used for pin path generation and logging\n- `mapType`: Type of BPF map (Hash, LRUHash, PerCPUHash, etc.)\n- `mapKey`: Sample key implementing `MapKey` interface (used for size and type info)\n- `mapValue`: Sample value implementing `MapValue` interface\n- `maxEntries`: Maximum number of entries the map can hold\n- `flags`: BPF map flags (e.g., `BPF_F_NO_PREALLOC`)\n\n**Returns:** A new `Map` instance configured but not yet created. You must call `Open()`, `OpenOrCreate()`, or `Create()` to actually create the map.\n\n**Semantics:**\n- The map is not pinned to the filesystem until explicitly opened\n- `mapKey` and `mapValue` are used only to determine sizes; they are not stored\n- The returned `Map` must be opened before it can be used for CRUD operations\n\n#### NewMapWithInnerSpec\n\nCreates a new `Map` with an inner map specification, used for map-of-maps.\n\n```go\nfunc NewMapWithInnerSpec(\n    name string,\n    mapType ebpf.MapType,\n    mapKey MapKey,\n    mapValue MapValue,\n    maxEntries int,\n    flags uint32,\n    innerSpec *ebpf.MapSpec,\n) *Map\n```\n\nSimilar to `NewMap()`, but includes an `innerSpec` for inner map configuration.\n\n#### OpenMap\n\nOpens a map that was previously pinned to the filesystem.\n\n```go\nfunc OpenMap(pinPath string, key MapKey, value MapValue) (*Map, error)\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `pinPath`: Absolute path to the pinned map file\n- `key`: Sample key of the map\n- `value`: Sample value of the map\n\n**Returns:** An opened `Map` or an error if the map doesn't exist or is incompatible.\n\n**Errors:**\n- Returns error if `pinPath` is not absolute\n- Returns error if the map file doesn't exist at the pin path\n- Returns error if the map is incompatible with the provided key/value types\n\n**Semantics:**\n- The map must already exist at the pin path\n- The opened map is immediately ready for CRUD operations\n- The key and value types are verified against the pinned map\n\n### Map Lifecycle Operations\n\n#### OpenOrCreate\n\nOpens the map if it exists and is compatible, or creates it if it doesn't. If the existing map's attributes (type, key/value size, capacity, flags) don't match, the map will be deleted and recreated.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) OpenOrCreate() error\n```\n\n**Returns:** Error if the operation fails.\n\n**Semantics:**\n- If the map is incompatible, it is deleted and recreated without retaining previous contents\n- Maps are pinned to the filesystem by default\n- Non-persistent maps are always recreated\n- The map's path is automatically determined from its name if not set\n- Safe to call multiple times (idempotent)\n- Must hold write lock (internal)\n\n**Example usage:**\n```go\nm := NewMap(\"my_map\", ebpf.Hash, &TestKey{}, &TestValue{}, 10000, 0)\nif err := m.OpenOrCreate(); err != nil {\n    // Handle error\n}\ndefer m.Close()\n```\n\n#### CreateUnpinned\n\nCreates the map without pinning it to the filesystem. The map exists only in kernel memory for the lifetime of the process.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) CreateUnpinned() error\n```\n\n**Returns:** Error if creation fails.\n\n**Semantics:**\n- The map is created in the kernel but not persisted to the filesystem\n- The map will be destroyed when the process exits or the map is closed\n- Useful for temporary maps or maps that don't need persistence across restarts\n- Cannot be called on an already-open map\n\n#### Create\n\nSimilar to `OpenOrCreate()` but closes the map immediately after creating or opening it.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Create() error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Calls `OpenOrCreate()` then immediately `Close()`\n- Useful for maps that are only needed to exist on the filesystem but not actively used\n- After `Create()` returns, the map is no longer open in the current process\n\n#### Recreate\n\nRemoves any existing pin and recreates the map from scratch, then re-pins it.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Recreate() error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Deletes the pinned map at the map's path\n- Creates the map fresh in the kernel\n- Re-pins the new map to the filesystem\n- All previous map entries are lost\n- Useful for resetting a map to an empty state\n- Returns error if the map is already open\n\n#### Open\n\nOpens an existing pinned map. The map must have been previously created and pinned.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Open() error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Loads a pinned map from the filesystem\n- The map must exist at the path determined from the map's name\n- Safe to call multiple times (idempotent)\n- After successful open, the map is ready for CRUD operations\n\n#### Close\n\nCloses the map and releases kernel resources.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Close() error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Closes the kernel file descriptor\n- If sync is enabled (via `WithCache()`), cancels the error resolver controller\n- The map persists on the filesystem if it was pinned\n- Safe to call on an already-closed map\n- After close, CRUD operations will return an error until the map is reopened\n\n#### IsOpen\n\nReturns whether the map is currently open.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) IsOpen() bool\n```\n\n### Builder Pattern Methods\n\nThese methods enable fluent configuration of maps before creation.\n\n#### WithCache\n\nEnables local caching of all entries inserted from user space. Useful for tracking synchronization status and detecting errors.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) WithCache() *Map\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Maintains an in-memory cache of all map entries and their sync status\n- Enables the error resolver, which periodically retries failed operations\n- Returns `m` for chaining\n\n#### WithEvents\n\nEnables an event buffer that records map operations (add/update/delete) for auditing and debugging.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) WithEvents(c option.BPFEventBufferConfig) *Map\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `c.Enabled`: Whether to enable the event buffer\n- `c.MaxSize`: Maximum number of events to retain\n- `c.TTL`: How long to keep events before garbage collection\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Creates a bounded ring buffer of recent map events\n- Events older than TTL are periodically garbage collected\n- Approximates 100MB per million capacity entries\n- Returns `m` for chaining\n\n#### WithGroupName\n\nSets the metric group name for this map (for grouping metrics).\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) WithGroupName(group string) *Map\n```\n\n#### WithPressureMetricThreshold\n\nEnables tracking of map pressure (fullness) when pressure exceeds a threshold.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) WithPressureMetricThreshold(registry *metrics.Registry, threshold float64) *Map\n```\n\n#### WithPressureMetric\n\nEnables tracking of map pressure with threshold 0 (always report).\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) WithPressureMetric(registry *metrics.Registry) *Map\n```\n\n### Accessor Methods\n\n#### Name\n\nReturns the basename of the map.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Name() string\n```\n\n#### Path\n\nReturns the filesystem path where the map is (or will be) pinned.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Path) Path() (string, error)\n```\n\n**Returns:** The pin path or an error if the path cannot be determined.\n\n#### FD\n\nReturns the underlying kernel file descriptor.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) FD() int\n```\n\n#### Type\n\nReturns the BPF map type.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Type() ebpf.MapType\n```\n\n#### KeySize\n\nReturns the size of map keys in bytes.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) KeySize() uint32\n```\n\n#### ValueSize\n\nReturns the size of map values in bytes.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) ValueSize() uint32\n```\n\n#### MaxEntries\n\nReturns the maximum number of entries the map can hold.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) MaxEntries() uint32\n```\n\n#### Flags\n\nReturns the BPF map flags.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Flags() uint32\n```\n\n## CRUD Operations\n\n### Lookup\n\nRetrieves a value from the map by key.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Lookup(key MapKey) (MapValue, error)\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `key`: Key to look up\n\n**Returns:** A new instance of the map's value type, or error if not found.\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Returns a new value instance (not a reference to internal data)\n- Safe to retain returned values\n- Returns error if the key is not in the map\n- Opens the map automatically if not already open\n\n**Example:**\n```go\nvalue, err := m.Lookup(&MyKey{ID: 42})\nif err != nil {\n    // Key not found or error occurred\n}\n```\n\n### Update\n\nInserts or updates a key-value pair in the map.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Update(key MapKey, value MapValue) error\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `key`: Key to insert/update\n- `value`: Value to associate with the key\n\n**Returns:** Error if the operation fails.\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Creates a new entry if the key doesn't exist\n- Overwrites the value if the key exists\n- Automatically opens the map if not already open\n- Updates local cache if enabled\n- Adds event to event buffer if enabled\n- On error, schedules the error resolver to retry\n\n**Example:**\n```go\nif err := m.Update(&MyKey{ID: 42}, &MyValue{Data: \"hello\"}); err != nil {\n    log.Fatal(err)\n}\n```\n\n### Delete\n\nDeletes a key-value pair from the map.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Delete(key MapKey) error\n```\n\n**Returns:** Error if the operation fails or if the key doesn't exist.\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Removes the entry if it exists\n- Returns an error if the key is not found\n- Updates local cache if enabled\n- Adds event to event buffer if enabled\n- On error, schedules the error resolver to retry\n\n#### SilentDelete\n\nDeletes a key from the map, returning silently if the key doesn't exist.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) SilentDelete(key MapKey) (deleted bool, err error)\n```\n\n**Returns:** `(true, nil)` if deleted, `(false, nil)` if key doesn't exist, or error on failure.\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Unlike `Delete()`, does not return an error if the key is missing\n- Returns `false` if the key wasn't in the map\n- Useful for best-effort cleanup\n\n#### DeleteLocked\n\nDeletes a key from the map. **Must be called from within a `DumpCallback` to avoid deadlocks.**\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) DeleteLocked(key MapKey) error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Assumes the map's write lock is already held\n- Should only be called from within a `DumpCallback` passed to `DumpReliablyWithCallback()`\n- Attempting to call from outside a callback while the map is being dumped will cause a deadlock\n\n**Example:**\n```go\nm.DumpReliablyWithCallback(func(key MapKey, value MapValue) {\n    if shouldDelete(key) {\n        m.DeleteLocked(key)  // Safe here\n    }\n}, stats)\n```\n\n### DeleteAll\n\nDeletes all entries from the map.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) DeleteAll() error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Iterates through the map and deletes each entry individually\n- If entries are added during deletion, they may not be deleted\n- Updates cache for each deletion\n- Returns error if any deletion fails\n- Updates pressure metric when complete\n\n### ClearAll\n\nClears all entries in a map by overwriting them with empty values.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) ClearAll() error\n```\n\n**Errors:**\n- Returns error if the map has events enabled\n- Returns error if the map has value cache enabled\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Different from `DeleteAll()`: overwrites entries instead of deleting them\n- Used in scenarios where overwriting is more efficient than deletion\n- Not compatible with event or cache buffers\n\n### Batch Lookup\n\nRetrieves multiple key-value pairs efficiently using the BPF batch API.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) BatchLookup(\n    cursor *ebpf.MapBatchCursor,\n    keysOut, valuesOut any,\n    opts *ebpf.BatchOptions,\n) (int, error)\n```\n\n**Returns:** Number of entries retrieved and any error.\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Uses the kernel's batch lookup API for more efficient iteration\n- Cursor state is preserved across calls\n- Low-level operation; typically used via `BatchIterator`\n\n### Per-CPU Operations\n\n#### DumpPerCPUWithCallback\n\nIterates over all entries in a per-CPU map.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) DumpPerCPUWithCallback(cb DumpPerCPUCallback) error\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `cb`: Callback invoked for each map entry with the key and slice of per-CPU values\n\n**Type:**\n```go\ntype DumpPerCPUCallback func(key MapKey, values any)\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- For each entry, `values` is a slice of `MapPerCPUValue` containing one value per CPU\n- Map must be a per-CPU map type (PerCPUHash, PerCPUArray, LRUCPUHash, PerCPUCGroupStorage)\n- Value type must implement `MapPerCPUValue` interface\n- Returns error if the map is not a per-CPU type or value doesn't implement the interface\n- Returns fresh instances on each callback (safe to retain values)\n\n## Iteration and Dumping\n\n### Basic Iteration\n\n#### DumpWithCallback\n\nIterates over all entries in the map, invoking a callback for each entry.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) DumpWithCallback(cb DumpCallback) error\n```\n\n**Type:**\n```go\ntype DumpCallback func(key MapKey, value MapValue)\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Opens the map automatically if not already open\n- Callback is invoked once for each entry\n- Returned values are fresh instances (safe to retain)\n- Returns error if callback is nil\n- Returns error on iteration failure\n\n**Example:**\n```go\nm.DumpWithCallback(func(key MapKey, value MapValue) {\n    log.Printf(\"Key: %v, Value: %v\", key, value)\n})\n```\n\n#### DumpWithCallbackIfExists\n\nLike `DumpWithCallback`, but returns silently if the map doesn't exist on the filesystem.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) DumpWithCallbackIfExists(cb DumpCallback) error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Returns `nil` if the map file doesn't exist\n- Otherwise identical to `DumpWithCallback`\n\n#### DumpReliablyWithCallback\n\nRobustly iterates over a map that may be concurrently modified, with tracking of iteration progress and recovery from concurrent deletions.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) DumpReliablyWithCallback(\n    cb DumpCallback,\n    stats *DumpStats,\n) error\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `cb`: Callback invoked for each entry\n- `stats`: Statistics object (initialized via `NewDumpStats()`) tracking iteration state\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Handles entries being deleted during iteration by backtracking to a previously seen key\n- Caps iteration at 4× the maximum map size to prevent infinite loops\n- Returns `ErrMaxLookup` if the limit is exceeded\n- Callback must not invoke map operations that require the write lock\n- Holds the write lock during iteration (to allow deletions within callbacks)\n- Populates `stats` with iteration statistics (lookups, failures, etc.)\n- Returns `nil` and `stats.Completed == true` when fully iterated\n- Returns `ErrMaxLookup` if iteration limit exceeded without completing\n\n**Statistics Tracking:**\n```go\ntype DumpStats struct {\n    Started          time.Time  // Iteration start time\n    Finished         time.Time  // Iteration finish time\n    Lookup           uint32     // Number of key lookups\n    LookupFailed     uint32     // Failed lookups\n    KeyFallback      uint32     // Fallbacks to previous key\n    MaxEntries       uint32     // Map capacity\n    Interrupted      uint32     // Iteration restarts\n    Completed        bool       // Whether fully iterated\n}\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```go\nstats := NewDumpStats(m)\nerr := m.DumpReliablyWithCallback(func(key MapKey, value MapValue) {\n    // Process entry\n}, stats)\nif err != nil {\n    log.Printf(\"Iteration error: %v\", err)\n}\nlog.Printf(\"Completed: %v, Lookups: %d, Duration: %v\",\n    stats.Completed, stats.Lookup, stats.Duration())\n```\n\n### Simple Dump\n\n#### Dump\n\nDumps the entire map into a Go map (string -> []string).\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Dump(hash map[string][]string) error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Keys are converted to strings and used as map keys\n- Values are converted to strings and appended to slices\n- Useful for debugging and testing\n- Returns error on failure\n\n#### DumpIfExists\n\nLike `Dump`, but returns silently if the map doesn't exist.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) DumpIfExists(hash map[string][]string) error\n```\n\n### Batch Iterator\n\n`BatchIterator` provides a typed, convenient interface for iterating maps using the BPF batch API.\n\n```go\ntype BatchIterator[KT, VT any, KP KeyPointer[KT], VP ValuePointer[VT]] struct {\n    // ... internal fields\n}\n```\n\n**Creating an Iterator:**\n```go\nfunc NewBatchIterator[KT any, VT any, KP KeyPointer[KT], VP ValuePointer[VT]](\n    m *Map,\n) *BatchIterator[KT, VT, KP, VP]\n```\n\n**Iterating:**\n```go\niter := NewBatchIterator[TestKey, TestValue](m)\nfor key, value := range iter.IterateAll(ctx) {\n    // Process key and value\n}\nif err := iter.Err(); err != nil {\n    // Handle iteration error\n}\n```\n\n**Type Constraints:**\n- `KT`: Key value type (e.g., `TestKey`)\n- `VT`: Value type (e.g., `TestValue`)\n- `KP`: Pointer type of key (e.g., `*TestKey`) - must implement `MapKey`\n- `VP`: Pointer type of value (e.g., `*TestValue`) - must implement `MapValue`\n\n#### IterateAll\n\nReturns a sequence for iterating all map entries.\n\n```go\nfunc (bi *BatchIterator[...]) IterateAll(\n    ctx context.Context,\n    opts ...BatchIteratorOpt[...],\n) iter.Seq2[KP, VP]\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Automatically handles ENOSPC errors by doubling buffer size and retrying\n- Supports up to 3 retries by default (configurable)\n- Context can be used to cancel iteration\n- Returns a `Seq2` that can be used in `for` loops\n- Resets internal state on each call (can be reused)\n- Only supports Hash, LRUHash, and LPMTrie map types\n- Returns error via `Err()` if iteration fails\n\n**Buffer Size Handling:**\n- Initial buffer size is calculated from `sqrt(max_entries * 2)`\n- Doubles on ENOSPC until maximum retries exhausted\n- Cursor position is preserved on ENOSPC, allowing retry at the same position\n\n#### Err\n\nReturns any error encountered during the most recent iteration.\n\n```go\nfunc (bi BatchIterator[...]) Err() error\n```\n\n#### Options\n\nOptions for customizing iterator behavior:\n\n```go\nfunc WithMaxRetries[...](retries uint32) BatchIteratorOpt[...]\nfunc WithStartingChunkSize[...](size int) BatchIteratorOpt[...]\nfunc WithEBPFBatchOpts[...](opts *ebpf.BatchOptions) BatchIteratorOpt[...]\n```\n\n**Example with options:**\n```go\niter := NewBatchIterator[TestKey, TestValue](m)\nfor k, v := range iter.IterateAll(ctx,\n    WithMaxRetries(5),\n    WithStartingChunkSize(1024),\n) {\n    // Process\n}\n```\n\n#### Helper Functions\n\n```go\n// Count all entries using batch iterator\nfunc CountAll[...](ctx context.Context, iter *BatchIterator[...]) (int, error)\n```\n\n## Pinning and Persistence\n\n### Filesystem Paths\n\n#### BPFFSRoot\n\nReturns the root path of the mounted BPF filesystem.\n\n```go\nfunc BPFFSRoot() string\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Typically `/sys/fs/bpf` on standard systems\n- May be `/run/cilium/bpffs` in containerized environments\n- Locked after first access (prevents changes during runtime)\n\n#### CiliumPath\n\nReturns the Cilium-specific base path for pinned eBPF objects.\n\n```go\nfunc CiliumPath() string\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Returns `<BPFFSRoot>/cilium`\n- Base directory for all Cilium eBPF pins\n\n#### MapPath\n\nReturns the filesystem path for a map with the given name.\n\n```go\nfunc MapPath(logger *slog.Logger, name string) string\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Returns `<CiliumPath()>/<name>` for Cilium agent\n- Computes path from mount info for other components\n- Logger used for fatal errors during mount detection\n\n#### TCGlobalsPath\n\nReturns the path to the TC globals directory (legacy pin paths).\n\n```go\nfunc TCGlobalsPath() string\n```\n\n### Pin/Unpin Operations\n\n#### Unpin\n\nRemoves the map from the filesystem.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Unpin() error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Deletes the pin file on the filesystem\n- The map remains open in the kernel (if currently open)\n- Returns error if the pin path cannot be determined\n\n#### UnpinIfExists\n\nUnpins the map only if it exists.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) UnpinIfExists() error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Returns `nil` if the map doesn't exist on the filesystem\n- Otherwise identical to `Unpin()`\n- Useful for cleanup operations that shouldn't fail on missing maps\n\n### Map Persistence Behavior\n\n**Pinned Maps** (created via `OpenOrCreate()` or `Create()` without `CreateUnpinned()`):\n- Persisted to the BPF filesystem at pin path\n- Survive process restarts\n- Can be loaded via `OpenMap()` or `Open()`\n- Automatically loaded during `OpenOrCreate()` if compatible\n\n**Unpinned Maps** (created via `CreateUnpinned()`):\n- Exist only in kernel memory\n- Destroyed when process exits or map is closed\n- Cannot be accessed from other processes\n- Useful for temporary per-process maps\n\n**Map Compatibility:**\n- When opening a pinned map via `OpenOrCreate()`, map attributes are checked\n- If incompatible (type, key/value size, capacity differs), the old map is deleted and recreated\n- Incompatibility causes loss of previous map contents\n\n## Key/Value Interfaces\n\n### MapKey Interface\n\nAll map keys must implement the `MapKey` interface.\n\n```go\ntype MapKey interface {\n    fmt.Stringer\n    // New must return a pointer to a new MapKey of the same type.\n    New() MapKey\n}\n```\n\n**Requirements:**\n- Must be a pointer type (e.g., `*MyKey`)\n- Must implement `String()` for string representation\n- Must implement `New()` to create new zero-initialized instances\n- Size must be deterministic (used for MapSpec)\n\n**Example:**\n```go\ntype EndpointKey struct {\n    IP        types.IPv6\n    Family    uint8\n    Key       uint8\n    ClusterID uint16\n}\n\nfunc (k *EndpointKey) String() string {\n    // Return string representation\n}\n\nfunc (k *EndpointKey) New() MapKey {\n    return &EndpointKey{}\n}\n```\n\n### MapValue Interface\n\nAll map values must implement the `MapValue` interface.\n\n```go\ntype MapValue interface {\n    fmt.Stringer\n    // New must return a pointer to a new MapValue of the same type.\n    New() MapValue\n}\n```\n\n**Requirements:**\n- Must be a pointer type (e.g., `*MyValue`)\n- Must implement `String()` for string representation\n- Must implement `New()` to create new zero-initialized instances\n- Size must be deterministic (used for MapSpec)\n\n**Example:**\n```go\ntype EndpointValue struct {\n    IfIndex uint32\n    Unused  uint32\n}\n\nfunc (v *EndpointValue) String() string {\n    return fmt.Sprintf(\"ifindex=%d\", v.IfIndex)\n}\n\nfunc (v *EndpointValue) New() MapValue {\n    return &EndpointValue{}\n}\n```\n\n### MapPerCPUValue Interface\n\nFor per-CPU maps, values must implement `MapPerCPUValue`.\n\n```go\ntype MapPerCPUValue interface {\n    MapValue\n    // NewSlice returns a pointer to a slice of structs implementing MapValue.\n    NewSlice() any\n}\n```\n\n**Requirements:**\n- Must also implement `MapValue`\n- Must implement `NewSlice()` returning a pointer to a slice of values\n- Slice contains one element per CPU on the system\n\n**Example:**\n```go\ntype PerCPUStats struct {\n    Packets uint64\n    Bytes   uint64\n}\n\nfunc (s *PerCPUStats) NewSlice() any {\n    return &[]PerCPUStats{}\n}\n```\n\n### Concrete Example: EndpointKey\n\nThe `EndpointKey` type demonstrates the required implementation:\n\n```go\ntype EndpointKey struct {\n    IP        types.IPv6  // IPv6 address (IPv4 in lower 4 bytes)\n    Family    uint8       // EndpointKeyIPv4 (1) or EndpointKeyIPv6 (2)\n    Key       uint8       // Additional key field\n    ClusterID uint16      // Cluster identifier\n}\n\n// String returns \"IP:Key\" representation (e.g., \"10.0.0.1:0\")\nfunc (k EndpointKey) String() string { ... }\n\n// New returns a pointer to a new zero-initialized EndpointKey\nfunc (k EndpointKey) New() MapKey { ... }\n\n// NewEndpointKey convenience constructor\nfunc NewEndpointKey(addr netip.Addr, clusterID uint16) EndpointKey { ... }\n\n// ToAddr converts back to a network address\nfunc (k EndpointKey) ToAddr() netip.Addr { ... }\n```\n\n## Event System\n\nThe event system tracks map operations for auditing and debugging.\n\n### Action Type\n\nDescribes the type of map operation.\n\n```go\ntype Action uint8\n\nconst (\n    MapUpdate   Action = iota  // Key-value pair added/updated\n    MapDelete                  // Key deleted\n    MapDeleteAll               // All entries deleted at once\n)\n\nfunc (a Action) String() string  // \"update\", \"delete\", \"delete-all\"\n```\n\n### Event Type\n\nRepresents a single map operation event.\n\n```go\ntype Event struct {\n    Timestamp   time.Time\n    action      Action       // Use GetAction()\n    Key         MapKey       // The affected key\n    Value       MapValue     // The new value (nil for deletes)\n    DesiredAction DesiredAction\n    LastError   error\n}\n\n// Accessors\nfunc (e *Event) GetAction() string\nfunc (e Event) GetKey() string\nfunc (e Event) GetValue() string\nfunc (e Event) GetLastError() error\nfunc (e Event) GetDesiredAction() DesiredAction\n```\n\n### Event Subscription\n\n#### DumpAndSubscribe\n\nDumps existing buffered events and subscribes to future events.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) DumpAndSubscribe(\n    ctx context.Context,\n    callback EventCallbackFunc,\n    follow bool,\n)\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `ctx`: Context for event subscription lifetime\n- `callback`: Called for each event; if nil, only retrieves buffered events\n- `follow`: If true, continues observing new events; if false, only dumps existing\n\n**Type:**\n```go\ntype EventCallbackFunc func(Event)\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Dumping and subscription happen atomically (no events lost between operations)\n- If `callback` is nil, buffer is dumped but no subscription is created\n- If `follow` is false, buffer is dumped and subscription ends\n- If `follow` is true, subscription continues until context is canceled\n- Events are stored in a bounded ring buffer; old events are evicted when full\n\n**Example:**\n```go\nctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())\ndefer cancel()\n\nm.DumpAndSubscribe(ctx, func(e Event) {\n    log.Printf(\"[%s] %s -> %s\", e.GetAction(), e.GetKey(), e.GetValue())\n}, true)  // Follow new events\n\n// Process events until cancel() is called\n```\n\n#### IsEventsEnabled\n\nChecks if event buffering is enabled for the map.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) IsEventsEnabled() bool\n```\n\n**Returns:** True if events are being recorded.\n\n## Collection Loading\n\n`LoadCollection` and `LoadAndAssign` load compiled eBPF ELF files into the kernel and manage the resulting maps and programs.\n\n### CollectionOptions\n\nConfiguration for collection loading.\n\n```go\ntype CollectionOptions struct {\n    ebpf.CollectionOptions\n\n    // Replacements for datapath runtime configs (DECLARE_CONFIG)\n    Constants any\n\n    // Maps to rename during loading\n    MapRenames []map[string]string\n\n    // Inner maps to replace\n    MapReplacements map[string]*Map\n\n    // Objects to keep during reachability pruning\n    Keep *set.Set[string]\n\n    // Path to dump constants to (for sysdumps)\n    ConfigDumpPath string\n}\n```\n\n### LoadCollection\n\nLoads an eBPF collection spec into the kernel.\n\n```go\nfunc LoadCollection(\n    logger *slog.Logger,\n    spec *ebpf.CollectionSpec,\n    opts *CollectionOptions,\n) (*ebpf.Collection, func() error, error)\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `logger`: For logging during load\n- `spec`: The eBPF collection specification\n- `opts`: Load options (can be nil for defaults)\n\n**Returns:**\n- `*ebpf.Collection`: The loaded collection\n- `func() error`: Commit function (must be called after programs are attached)\n- `error`: Load error\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Maps marked as pinned are automatically loaded from the pin path if they exist\n- Reachability analysis prunes unused maps and programs\n- Tail calls are resolved and populated into the calls map\n- Runtime constants (DECLARE_CONFIG) are applied to the spec\n- Maps can be renamed before loading\n- Returns a commit function that must be called after attaching all entrypoint programs\n- The commit function finalizes map pins for maps marked as needing replacement\n\n**Important:** The returned `commit()` function **must** be called after all entrypoint programs from the collection are attached to their kernel hooks. This ensures tail call maps are properly initialized before the kernel runs the programs.\n\n**Example:**\n```go\ncoll, commit, err := LoadCollection(logger, spec, opts)\nif err != nil {\n    return err\n}\ndefer coll.Close()\n\n// Attach programs to hooks\ncoll.Programs[\"ingress\"].Attach(...)\ncoll.Programs[\"egress\"].Attach(...)\n\n// Finalize pins\nif err := commit(); err != nil {\n    return err\n}\n```\n\n### LoadAndAssign\n\nLoads a collection and assigns the programs and maps to fields in a struct.\n\n```go\nfunc LoadAndAssign(\n    logger *slog.Logger,\n    to any,\n    spec *ebpf.CollectionSpec,\n    opts *CollectionOptions,\n) (func() error, error)\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `logger`: For logging\n- `to`: Pointer to struct with fields for programs and maps\n- `spec`: The collection spec\n- `opts`: Load options\n\n**Returns:**\n- `func() error`: Commit function (same as LoadCollection)\n- `error`: Load or assignment error\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Automatically analyzes the target struct to determine which objects to keep\n- Assigns programs and maps to matching exported fields by name\n- Unknown objects in the collection are pruned\n- Like `LoadCollection`, the returned commit function must be called after attaching programs\n\n**Example:**\n```go\ntype DatapathObjects struct {\n    IngresProgram   *ebpf.Program `ebpf:\"ingress\"`\n    EgressProgram   *ebpf.Program `ebpf:\"egress\"`\n    ConnectionsMap  *Map          `ebpf:\"connections\"`\n}\n\nobjs := &DatapathObjects{}\ncommit, err := LoadAndAssign(logger, objs, spec, opts)\nif err != nil {\n    return err\n}\n\n// Attach programs\nobjs.IngresProgram.Attach(...)\nobjs.EgressProgram.Attach(...)\n\n// Finalize\nreturn commit()\n```\n\n## Usage Examples\n\n### Basic Map Creation and CRUD\n\n```go\npackage main\n\nimport (\n    \"log\"\n    \"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/bpf\"\n    \"github.com/cilium/ebpf\"\n)\n\ntype MyKey struct {\n    ID uint32\n}\n\nfunc (k *MyKey) String() string {\n    return fmt.Sprintf(\"ID:%d\", k.ID)\n}\n\nfunc (k *MyKey) New() bpf.MapKey {\n    return &MyKey{}\n}\n\ntype MyValue struct {\n    Count uint64\n}\n\nfunc (v *MyValue) String() string {\n    return fmt.Sprintf(\"Count:%d\", v.Count)\n}\n\nfunc (v *MyValue) New() bpf.MapValue {\n    return &MyValue{}\n}\n\nfunc main() {\n    // Create map\n    m := bpf.NewMap(\"my_map\", ebpf.Hash, &MyKey{}, &MyValue{}, 10000, 0)\n\n    // Open or create the map\n    if err := m.OpenOrCreate(); err != nil {\n        log.Fatalf(\"Failed to create map: %v\", err)\n    }\n    defer m.Close()\n\n    // Insert\n    key := &MyKey{ID: 42}\n    value := &MyValue{Count: 100}\n    if err := m.Update(key, value); err != nil {\n        log.Fatalf(\"Update failed: %v\", err)\n    }\n\n    // Lookup\n    retrieved, err := m.Lookup(key)\n    if err != nil {\n        log.Fatalf(\"Lookup failed: %v\", err)\n    }\n    log.Printf(\"Retrieved: %v\", retrieved)\n\n    // Delete\n    if err := m.Delete(key); err != nil {\n        log.Fatalf(\"Delete failed: %v\", err)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Iteration with DumpWithCallback\n\n```go\nfunc dumpMap(m *bpf.Map) error {\n    return m.DumpWithCallback(func(key bpf.MapKey, value bpf.MapValue) {\n        log.Printf(\"  %s -> %s\", key.String(), value.String())\n    })\n}\n```\n\n### Reliable Iteration with Recovery\n\n```go\nfunc reliableIterateMap(m *bpf.Map) error {\n    stats := bpf.NewDumpStats(m)\n\n    err := m.DumpReliablyWithCallback(func(key bpf.MapKey, value bpf.MapValue) {\n        log.Printf(\"  %s -> %s\", key.String(), value.String())\n    }, stats)\n\n    if err != nil && err != bpf.ErrMaxLookup {\n        return err\n    }\n\n    log.Printf(\"Iteration stats: lookups=%d, failures=%d, completed=%v, duration=%v\",\n        stats.Lookup, stats.LookupFailed, stats.Completed, stats.Duration())\n\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\n### Batch Iterator\n\n```go\nfunc iterateWithBatch(ctx context.Context, m *bpf.Map) error {\n    iter := bpf.NewBatchIterator[MyKey, MyValue](m)\n\n    count := 0\n    for key, value := range iter.IterateAll(ctx) {\n        log.Printf(\"  %s -> %s\", key.String(), value.String())\n        count++\n    }\n\n    if err := iter.Err(); err != nil {\n        log.Printf(\"Iteration error: %v\", err)\n        return err\n    }\n\n    log.Printf(\"Iterated %d entries\", count)\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\n### Event Subscription\n\n```go\nfunc subscribeToEvents(ctx context.Context, m *bpf.Map) {\n    m.DumpAndSubscribe(ctx, func(event bpf.Event) {\n        log.Printf(\"[%s] %s -> %s (error: %v)\",\n            event.GetAction(),\n            event.GetKey(),\n            event.GetValue(),\n            event.GetLastError())\n    }, true)  // follow future events\n\n    // Listen for events until context is canceled\n}\n```\n\n### Pinning and Unpinning\n\n```go\nfunc manageMapPins() error {\n    m := bpf.NewMap(\"shared_map\", ebpf.Hash, &MyKey{}, &MyValue{}, 10000, 0)\n\n    // Create and pin\n    if err := m.OpenOrCreate(); err != nil {\n        return err\n    }\n    defer m.Close()\n\n    // Map is now pinned to the filesystem at <CiliumPath>/shared_map\n    path, _ := m.Path()\n    log.Printf(\"Map pinned to: %s\", path)\n\n    // Later, in another process, open the pinned map\n    m2, err := bpf.OpenMap(path, &MyKey{}, &MyValue{})\n    if err != nil {\n        return err\n    }\n    defer m2.Close()\n\n    // Unpin the map from the filesystem\n    if err := m2.Unpin(); err != nil {\n        return err\n    }\n\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\n### Collection Loading\n\n```go\nfunc loadDatapath(logger *slog.Logger) error {\n    // Load ELF file and parse spec\n    spec, err := ebpf.LoadCollectionSpec(\"bpf_program.o\")\n    if err != nil {\n        return err\n    }\n\n    opts := &bpf.CollectionOptions{\n        CollectionOptions: ebpf.CollectionOptions{\n            Programs: ebpf.ProgramOptions{\n                KernelTypes: btfSpec,\n            },\n            Maps: ebpf.MapOptions{\n                PinPath: bpf.CiliumPath(),\n            },\n        },\n    }\n\n    coll, commit, err := bpf.LoadCollection(logger, spec, opts)\n    if err != nil {\n        return err\n    }\n    defer coll.Close()\n\n    // Attach programs\n    if err := attachPrograms(coll); err != nil {\n        return err\n    }\n\n    // Finalize map pins\n    if err := commit(); err != nil {\n        return err\n    }\n\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\n### Deletion During Iteration\n\n```go\nfunc filterMap(m *bpf.Map, shouldDelete func(bpf.MapKey) bool) error {\n    stats := bpf.NewDumpStats(m)\n\n    return m.DumpReliablyWithCallback(func(key bpf.MapKey, value bpf.MapValue) {\n        if shouldDelete(key) {\n            // Safe to delete within the callback\n            if err := m.DeleteLocked(key); err != nil {\n                log.Printf(\"Delete failed: %v\", err)\n            }\n        }\n    }, stats)\n}\n```\n\n### Map with Cache and Events\n\n```go\nfunc setupMapWithTracking(logger *slog.Logger) (*bpf.Map, error) {\n    m := bpf.NewMap(\"tracked_map\", ebpf.Hash, &MyKey{}, &MyValue{}, 10000, 0).\n        WithCache().\n        WithEvents(option.BPFEventBufferConfig{\n            Enabled: true,\n            MaxSize: 1000,\n            TTL:     5 * time.Minute,\n        })\n\n    if err := m.OpenOrCreate(); err != nil {\n        return nil, err\n    }\n\n    // Subscribe to events\n    ctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())\n    go func() {\n        defer cancel()\n        m.DumpAndSubscribe(ctx, func(event bpf.Event) {\n            log.Printf(\"Event: %s\", event.GetAction())\n        }, true)\n    }()\n\n    return m, nil\n}\n```\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### Common Errors\n\n- **ErrMapNotOpened**: Returned when operations are attempted on a map that hasn't been opened\n- **ErrKeyNotExist**: Returned from Lookup when key doesn't exist (wrapped in ebpf errors)\n- **ErrMaxLookup**: Returned from DumpReliablyWithCallback when iteration limit exceeded\n- **ErrMapIncompatible**: Returned when LoadCollection encounters incompatible pinned maps\n\n### Synchronization and Error Recovery\n\nWhen a map has caching enabled via `WithCache()`, failed Update or Delete operations are tracked:\n\n1. The error is recorded in the cache entry\n2. An error resolver controller is scheduled\n3. The controller periodically retries failed operations\n4. Once resolved, the cache entry is updated to reflect the successful operation\n\nThis provides resilience against transient failures.\n\n## Design Patterns and Best Practices\n\n### Pattern: Stateful Map Operations with Caching\n\nUse `WithCache()` when you need to track synchronization state or ensure reliable operation delivery:\n\n```go\nm := bpf.NewMap(name, mapType, key, value, maxEntries, flags).\n    WithCache().\n    WithGroupName(\"my_maps\")\n\nm.OpenOrCreate()\n// Updates are tracked and retried on failure\n```\n\n### Pattern: Pinning Maps for Persistence\n\nMaps are pinned by default via `OpenOrCreate()`. To prevent pinning (for temporary maps), use `CreateUnpinned()`:\n\n```go\n// Persistent map (default)\nm := bpf.NewMap(name, ...)\nm.OpenOrCreate()  // Pinned at <CiliumPath>/name\n\n// Temporary map\nm2 := bpf.NewMap(name, ...)\nm2.CreateUnpinned()  // Not persisted, destroyed on process exit\n```\n\n### Pattern: Safe Concurrent Dumping with Deletion\n\nWhen dumping a map where entries may be modified concurrently, use `DumpReliablyWithCallback()` with `DeleteLocked()`:\n\n```go\nstats := bpf.NewDumpStats(m)\nm.DumpReliablyWithCallback(func(key bpf.MapKey, value bpf.MapValue) {\n    if isExpired(value) {\n        m.DeleteLocked(key)  // Safe here - holds lock\n    }\n}, stats)\n```\n\n### Pattern: Batch Processing Large Maps\n\nFor efficient iteration of very large maps, prefer `BatchIterator` over `DumpWithCallback`:\n\n```go\n// Efficient batch processing\niter := bpf.NewBatchIterator[K, V](m,\n    bpf.WithStartingChunkSize(4096))\n\nfor k, v := range iter.IterateAll(ctx) {\n    processEntry(k, v)\n}\n```\n\n### Pattern: Map Lifecycle in Agents\n\n1. Create and configure maps before datapath loading\n2. Call `OpenOrCreate()` on all maps\n3. Load eBPF collection after maps exist\n4. Call `commit()` after attaching programs\n5. Subscribe to events if needed\n6. Close maps on shutdown\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":318,"cache_read_input_tokens":78644,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":318},"output_tokens":8,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"1d121e01-6c54-464b-b457-0d878b9009e9","uuid":"fbb6d9a1-5415-4fc6-ae63-768c7f9b682e"}

The API provides Go wrappers for user-space interaction with kernel eBPF maps.\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Core Map Type and Creation](#core-map-type-and-creation)\n2. [CRUD Operations](#crud-operations)\n3. [Iteration and Dumping](#iteration-and-dumping)\n4. [Pinning and Persistence](#pinning-and-persistence)\n5. [Key/Value Interfaces](#keyvalue-interfaces)\n6. [Event System](#event-system)\n7. [Collection Loading](#collection-loading)\n8. [Usage Examples](#usage-examples)\n\n## Core Map Type and Creation\n\n### Map Type\n\nThe `Map` type represents a BPF map and provides all operations for user-space interaction with kernel eBPF maps.\n\n```go\ntype Map struct {\n    Logger *slog.Logger\n    // ... internal fields\n}\n```\n\n### Creating Maps\n\n#### NewMap\n\nCreates a new `Map` instance with the specified configuration. The map is not yet created in the kernel.\n\n```go\nfunc NewMap(\n    name string,\n    mapType ebpf.MapType,\n    mapKey MapKey,\n    mapValue MapValue,\n    maxEntries int,\n    flags uint32,\n) *Map\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `name`: The map name used for pin path generation and logging\n- `mapType`: Type of BPF map (Hash, LRUHash, PerCPUHash, etc.)\n- `mapKey`: Sample key implementing `MapKey` interface (used for size and type info)\n- `mapValue`: Sample value implementing `MapValue` interface\n- `maxEntries`: Maximum number of entries the map can hold\n- `flags`: BPF map flags (e.g., `BPF_F_NO_PREALLOC`)\n\n**Returns:** A new `Map` instance configured but not yet created. You must call `Open()`, `OpenOrCreate()`, or `Create()` to actually create the map.\n\n**Semantics:**\n- The map is not pinned to the filesystem until explicitly opened\n- `mapKey` and `mapValue` are used only to determine sizes; they are not stored\n- The returned `Map` must be opened before it can be used for CRUD operations\n\n#### NewMapWithInnerSpec\n\nCreates a new `Map` with an inner map specification, used for map-of-maps.\n\n```go\nfunc NewMapWithInnerSpec(\n    name string,\n    mapType ebpf.MapType,\n    mapKey MapKey,\n    mapValue MapValue,\n    maxEntries int,\n    flags uint32,\n    innerSpec *ebpf.MapSpec,\n) *Map\n```\n\nSimilar to `NewMap()`, but includes an `innerSpec` for inner map configuration.\n\n#### OpenMap\n\nOpens a map that was previously pinned to the filesystem.\n\n```go\nfunc OpenMap(pinPath string, key MapKey, value MapValue) (*Map, error)\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `pinPath`: Absolute path to the pinned map file\n- `key`: Sample key of the map\n- `value`: Sample value of the map\n\n**Returns:** An opened `Map` or an error if the map doesn't exist or is incompatible.\n\n**Errors:**\n- Returns error if `pinPath` is not absolute\n- Returns error if the map file doesn't exist at the pin path\n- Returns error if the map is incompatible with the provided key/value types\n\n**Semantics:**\n- The map must already exist at the pin path\n- The opened map is immediately ready for CRUD operations\n- The key and value types are verified against the pinned map\n\n### Map Lifecycle Operations\n\n#### OpenOrCreate\n\nOpens the map if it exists and is compatible, or creates it if it doesn't. If the existing map's attributes (type, key/value size, capacity, flags) don't match, the map will be deleted and recreated.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) OpenOrCreate() error\n```\n\n**Returns:** Error if the operation fails.\n\n**Semantics:**\n- If the map is incompatible, it is deleted and recreated without retaining previous contents\n- Maps are pinned to the filesystem by default\n- Non-persistent maps are always recreated\n- The map's path is automatically determined from its name if not set\n- Safe to call multiple times (idempotent)\n- Must hold write lock (internal)\n\n**Example usage:**\n```go\nm := NewMap(\"my_map\", ebpf.Hash, &TestKey{}, &TestValue{}, 10000, 0)\nif err := m.OpenOrCreate(); err != nil {\n    // Handle error\n}\ndefer m.Close()\n```\n\n#### CreateUnpinned\n\nCreates the map without pinning it to the filesystem. The map exists only in kernel memory for the lifetime of the process.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) CreateUnpinned() error\n```\n\n**Returns:** Error if creation fails.\n\n**Semantics:**\n- The map is created in the kernel but not persisted to the filesystem\n- The map will be destroyed when the process exits or the map is closed\n- Useful for temporary maps or maps that don't need persistence across restarts\n- Cannot be called on an already-open map\n\n#### Create\n\nSimilar to `OpenOrCreate()` but closes the map immediately after creating or opening it.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Create() error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Calls `OpenOrCreate()` then immediately `Close()`\n- Useful for maps that are only needed to exist on the filesystem but not actively used\n- After `Create()` returns, the map is no longer open in the current process\n\n#### Recreate\n\nRemoves any existing pin and recreates the map from scratch, then re-pins it.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Recreate() error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Deletes the pinned map at the map's path\n- Creates the map fresh in the kernel\n- Re-pins the new map to the filesystem\n- All previous map entries are lost\n- Useful for resetting a map to an empty state\n- Returns error if the map is already open\n\n#### Open\n\nOpens an existing pinned map. The map must have been previously created and pinned.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Open() error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Loads a pinned map from the filesystem\n- The map must exist at the path determined from the map's name\n- Safe to call multiple times (idempotent)\n- After successful open, the map is ready for CRUD operations\n\n#### Close\n\nCloses the map and releases kernel resources.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Close() error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Closes the kernel file descriptor\n- If sync is enabled (via `WithCache()`), cancels the error resolver controller\n- The map persists on the filesystem if it was pinned\n- Safe to call on an already-closed map\n- After close, CRUD operations will return an error until the map is reopened\n\n#### IsOpen\n\nReturns whether the map is currently open.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) IsOpen() bool\n```\n\n### Builder Pattern Methods\n\nThese methods enable fluent configuration of maps before creation.\n\n#### WithCache\n\nEnables local caching of all entries inserted from user space. Useful for tracking synchronization status and detecting errors.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) WithCache() *Map\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Maintains an in-memory cache of all map entries and their sync status\n- Enables the error resolver, which periodically retries failed operations\n- Returns `m` for chaining\n\n#### WithEvents\n\nEnables an event buffer that records map operations (add/update/delete) for auditing and debugging.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) WithEvents(c option.BPFEventBufferConfig) *Map\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `c.Enabled`: Whether to enable the event buffer\n- `c.MaxSize`: Maximum number of events to retain\n- `c.TTL`: How long to keep events before garbage collection\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Creates a bounded ring buffer of recent map events\n- Events older than TTL are periodically garbage collected\n- Approximates 100MB per million capacity entries\n- Returns `m` for chaining\n\n#### WithGroupName\n\nSets the metric group name for this map (for grouping metrics).\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) WithGroupName(group string) *Map\n```\n\n#### WithPressureMetricThreshold\n\nEnables tracking of map pressure (fullness) when pressure exceeds a threshold.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) WithPressureMetricThreshold(registry *metrics.Registry, threshold float64) *Map\n```\n\n#### WithPressureMetric\n\nEnables tracking of map pressure with threshold 0 (always report).\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) WithPressureMetric(registry *metrics.Registry) *Map\n```\n\n### Accessor Methods\n\n#### Name\n\nReturns the basename of the map.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Name() string\n```\n\n#### Path\n\nReturns the filesystem path where the map is (or will be) pinned.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Path) Path() (string, error)\n```\n\n**Returns:** The pin path or an error if the path cannot be determined.\n\n#### FD\n\nReturns the underlying kernel file descriptor.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) FD() int\n```\n\n#### Type\n\nReturns the BPF map type.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Type() ebpf.MapType\n```\n\n#### KeySize\n\nReturns the size of map keys in bytes.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) KeySize() uint32\n```\n\n#### ValueSize\n\nReturns the size of map values in bytes.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) ValueSize() uint32\n```\n\n#### MaxEntries\n\nReturns the maximum number of entries the map can hold.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) MaxEntries() uint32\n```\n\n#### Flags\n\nReturns the BPF map flags.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Flags() uint32\n```\n\n## CRUD Operations\n\n### Lookup\n\nRetrieves a value from the map by key.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Lookup(key MapKey) (MapValue, error)\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `key`: Key to look up\n\n**Returns:** A new instance of the map's value type, or error if not found.\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Returns a new value instance (not a reference to internal data)\n- Safe to retain returned values\n- Returns error if the key is not in the map\n- Opens the map automatically if not already open\n\n**Example:**\n```go\nvalue, err := m.Lookup(&MyKey{ID: 42})\nif err != nil {\n    // Key not found or error occurred\n}\n```\n\n### Update\n\nInserts or updates a key-value pair in the map.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Update(key MapKey, value MapValue) error\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `key`: Key to insert/update\n- `value`: Value to associate with the key\n\n**Returns:** Error if the operation fails.\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Creates a new entry if the key doesn't exist\n- Overwrites the value if the key exists\n- Automatically opens the map if not already open\n- Updates local cache if enabled\n- Adds event to event buffer if enabled\n- On error, schedules the error resolver to retry\n\n**Example:**\n```go\nif err := m.Update(&MyKey{ID: 42}, &MyValue{Data: \"hello\"}); err != nil {\n    log.Fatal(err)\n}\n```\n\n### Delete\n\nDeletes a key-value pair from the map.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Delete(key MapKey) error\n```\n\n**Returns:** Error if the operation fails or if the key doesn't exist.\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Removes the entry if it exists\n- Returns an error if the key is not found\n- Updates local cache if enabled\n- Adds event to event buffer if enabled\n- On error, schedules the error resolver to retry\n\n#### SilentDelete\n\nDeletes a key from the map, returning silently if the key doesn't exist.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) SilentDelete(key MapKey) (deleted bool, err error)\n```\n\n**Returns:** `(true, nil)` if deleted, `(false, nil)` if key doesn't exist, or error on failure.\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Unlike `Delete()`, does not return an error if the key is missing\n- Returns `false` if the key wasn't in the map\n- Useful for best-effort cleanup\n\n#### DeleteLocked\n\nDeletes a key from the map. **Must be called from within a `DumpCallback` to avoid deadlocks.**\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) DeleteLocked(key MapKey) error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Assumes the map's write lock is already held\n- Should only be called from within a `DumpCallback` passed to `DumpReliablyWithCallback()`\n- Attempting to call from outside a callback while the map is being dumped will cause a deadlock\n\n**Example:**\n```go\nm.DumpReliablyWithCallback(func(key MapKey, value MapValue) {\n    if shouldDelete(key) {\n        m.DeleteLocked(key)  // Safe here\n    }\n}, stats)\n```\n\n### DeleteAll\n\nDeletes all entries from the map.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) DeleteAll() error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Iterates through the map and deletes each entry individually\n- If entries are added during deletion, they may not be deleted\n- Updates cache for each deletion\n- Returns error if any deletion fails\n- Updates pressure metric when complete\n\n### ClearAll\n\nClears all entries in a map by overwriting them with empty values.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) ClearAll() error\n```\n\n**Errors:**\n- Returns error if the map has events enabled\n- Returns error if the map has value cache enabled\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Different from `DeleteAll()`: overwrites entries instead of deleting them\n- Used in scenarios where overwriting is more efficient than deletion\n- Not compatible with event or cache buffers\n\n### Batch Lookup\n\nRetrieves multiple key-value pairs efficiently using the BPF batch API.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) BatchLookup(\n    cursor *ebpf.MapBatchCursor,\n    keysOut, valuesOut any,\n    opts *ebpf.BatchOptions,\n) (int, error)\n```\n\n**Returns:** Number of entries retrieved and any error.\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Uses the kernel's batch lookup API for more efficient iteration\n- Cursor state is preserved across calls\n- Low-level operation; typically used via `BatchIterator`\n\n### Per-CPU Operations\n\n#### DumpPerCPUWithCallback\n\nIterates over all entries in a per-CPU map.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) DumpPerCPUWithCallback(cb DumpPerCPUCallback) error\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `cb`: Callback invoked for each map entry with the key and slice of per-CPU values\n\n**Type:**\n```go\ntype DumpPerCPUCallback func(key MapKey, values any)\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- For each entry, `values` is a slice of `MapPerCPUValue` containing one value per CPU\n- Map must be a per-CPU map type (PerCPUHash, PerCPUArray, LRUCPUHash, PerCPUCGroupStorage)\n- Value type must implement `MapPerCPUValue` interface\n- Returns error if the map is not a per-CPU type or value doesn't implement the interface\n- Returns fresh instances on each callback (safe to retain values)\n\n## Iteration and Dumping\n\n### Basic Iteration\n\n#### DumpWithCallback\n\nIterates over all entries in the map, invoking a callback for each entry.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) DumpWithCallback(cb DumpCallback) error\n```\n\n**Type:**\n```go\ntype DumpCallback func(key MapKey, value MapValue)\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Opens the map automatically if not already open\n- Callback is invoked once for each entry\n- Returned values are fresh instances (safe to retain)\n- Returns error if callback is nil\n- Returns error on iteration failure\n\n**Example:**\n```go\nm.DumpWithCallback(func(key MapKey, value MapValue) {\n    log.Printf(\"Key: %v, Value: %v\", key, value)\n})\n```\n\n#### DumpWithCallbackIfExists\n\nLike `DumpWithCallback`, but returns silently if the map doesn't exist on the filesystem.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) DumpWithCallbackIfExists(cb DumpCallback) error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Returns `nil` if the map file doesn't exist\n- Otherwise identical to `DumpWithCallback`\n\n#### DumpReliablyWithCallback\n\nRobustly iterates over a map that may be concurrently modified, with tracking of iteration progress and recovery from concurrent deletions.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) DumpReliablyWithCallback(\n    cb DumpCallback,\n    stats *DumpStats,\n) error\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `cb`: Callback invoked for each entry\n- `stats`: Statistics object (initialized via `NewDumpStats()`) tracking iteration state\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Handles entries being deleted during iteration by backtracking to a previously seen key\n- Caps iteration at 4× the maximum map size to prevent infinite loops\n- Returns `ErrMaxLookup` if the limit is exceeded\n- Callback must not invoke map operations that require the write lock\n- Holds the write lock during iteration (to allow deletions within callbacks)\n- Populates `stats` with iteration statistics (lookups, failures, etc.)\n- Returns `nil` and `stats.Completed == true` when fully iterated\n- Returns `ErrMaxLookup` if iteration limit exceeded without completing\n\n**Statistics Tracking:**\n```go\ntype DumpStats struct {\n    Started          time.Time  // Iteration start time\n    Finished         time.Time  // Iteration finish time\n    Lookup           uint32     // Number of key lookups\n    LookupFailed     uint32     // Failed lookups\n    KeyFallback      uint32     // Fallbacks to previous key\n    MaxEntries       uint32     // Map capacity\n    Interrupted      uint32     // Iteration restarts\n    Completed        bool       // Whether fully iterated\n}\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```go\nstats := NewDumpStats(m)\nerr := m.DumpReliablyWithCallback(func(key MapKey, value MapValue) {\n    // Process entry\n}, stats)\nif err != nil {\n    log.Printf(\"Iteration error: %v\", err)\n}\nlog.Printf(\"Completed: %v, Lookups: %d, Duration: %v\",\n    stats.Completed, stats.Lookup, stats.Duration())\n```\n\n### Simple Dump\n\n#### Dump\n\nDumps the entire map into a Go map (string -> []string).\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Dump(hash map[string][]string) error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Keys are converted to strings and used as map keys\n- Values are converted to strings and appended to slices\n- Useful for debugging and testing\n- Returns error on failure\n\n#### DumpIfExists\n\nLike `Dump`, but returns silently if the map doesn't exist.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) DumpIfExists(hash map[string][]string) error\n```\n\n### Batch Iterator\n\n`BatchIterator` provides a typed, convenient interface for iterating maps using the BPF batch API.\n\n```go\ntype BatchIterator[KT, VT any, KP KeyPointer[KT], VP ValuePointer[VT]] struct {\n    // ... internal fields\n}\n```\n\n**Creating an Iterator:**\n```go\nfunc NewBatchIterator[KT any, VT any, KP KeyPointer[KT], VP ValuePointer[VT]](\n    m *Map,\n) *BatchIterator[KT, VT, KP, VP]\n```\n\n**Iterating:**\n```go\niter := NewBatchIterator[TestKey, TestValue](m)\nfor key, value := range iter.IterateAll(ctx) {\n    // Process key and value\n}\nif err := iter.Err(); err != nil {\n    // Handle iteration error\n}\n```\n\n**Type Constraints:**\n- `KT`: Key value type (e.g., `TestKey`)\n- `VT`: Value type (e.g., `TestValue`)\n- `KP`: Pointer type of key (e.g., `*TestKey`) - must implement `MapKey`\n- `VP`: Pointer type of value (e.g., `*TestValue`) - must implement `MapValue`\n\n#### IterateAll\n\nReturns a sequence for iterating all map entries.\n\n```go\nfunc (bi *BatchIterator[...]) IterateAll(\n    ctx context.Context,\n    opts ...BatchIteratorOpt[...],\n) iter.Seq2[KP, VP]\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Automatically handles ENOSPC errors by doubling buffer size and retrying\n- Supports up to 3 retries by default (configurable)\n- Context can be used to cancel iteration\n- Returns a `Seq2` that can be used in `for` loops\n- Resets internal state on each call (can be reused)\n- Only supports Hash, LRUHash, and LPMTrie map types\n- Returns error via `Err()` if iteration fails\n\n**Buffer Size Handling:**\n- Initial buffer size is calculated from `sqrt(max_entries * 2)`\n- Doubles on ENOSPC until maximum retries exhausted\n- Cursor position is preserved on ENOSPC, allowing retry at the same position\n\n#### Err\n\nReturns any error encountered during the most recent iteration.\n\n```go\nfunc (bi BatchIterator[...]) Err() error\n```\n\n#### Options\n\nOptions for customizing iterator behavior:\n\n```go\nfunc WithMaxRetries[...](retries uint32) BatchIteratorOpt[...]\nfunc WithStartingChunkSize[...](size int) BatchIteratorOpt[...]\nfunc WithEBPFBatchOpts[...](opts *ebpf.BatchOptions) BatchIteratorOpt[...]\n```\n\n**Example with options:**\n```go\niter := NewBatchIterator[TestKey, TestValue](m)\nfor k, v := range iter.IterateAll(ctx,\n    WithMaxRetries(5),\n    WithStartingChunkSize(1024),\n) {\n    // Process\n}\n```\n\n#### Helper Functions\n\n```go\n// Count all entries using batch iterator\nfunc CountAll[...](ctx context.Context, iter *BatchIterator[...]) (int, error)\n```\n\n## Pinning and Persistence\n\n### Filesystem Paths\n\n#### BPFFSRoot\n\nReturns the root path of the mounted BPF filesystem.\n\n```go\nfunc BPFFSRoot() string\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Typically `/sys/fs/bpf` on standard systems\n- May be `/run/cilium/bpffs` in containerized environments\n- Locked after first access (prevents changes during runtime)\n\n#### CiliumPath\n\nReturns the Cilium-specific base path for pinned eBPF objects.\n\n```go\nfunc CiliumPath() string\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Returns `<BPFFSRoot>/cilium`\n- Base directory for all Cilium eBPF pins\n\n#### MapPath\n\nReturns the filesystem path for a map with the given name.\n\n```go\nfunc MapPath(logger *slog.Logger, name string) string\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Returns `<CiliumPath()>/<name>` for Cilium agent\n- Computes path from mount info for other components\n- Logger used for fatal errors during mount detection\n\n#### TCGlobalsPath\n\nReturns the path to the TC globals directory (legacy pin paths).\n\n```go\nfunc TCGlobalsPath() string\n```\n\n### Pin/Unpin Operations\n\n#### Unpin\n\nRemoves the map from the filesystem.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) Unpin() error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Deletes the pin file on the filesystem\n- The map remains open in the kernel (if currently open)\n- Returns error if the pin path cannot be determined\n\n#### UnpinIfExists\n\nUnpins the map only if it exists.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) UnpinIfExists() error\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Returns `nil` if the map doesn't exist on the filesystem\n- Otherwise identical to `Unpin()`\n- Useful for cleanup operations that shouldn't fail on missing maps\n\n### Map Persistence Behavior\n\n**Pinned Maps** (created via `OpenOrCreate()` or `Create()` without `CreateUnpinned()`):\n- Persisted to the BPF filesystem at pin path\n- Survive process restarts\n- Can be loaded via `OpenMap()` or `Open()`\n- Automatically loaded during `OpenOrCreate()` if compatible\n\n**Unpinned Maps** (created via `CreateUnpinned()`):\n- Exist only in kernel memory\n- Destroyed when process exits or map is closed\n- Cannot be accessed from other processes\n- Useful for temporary per-process maps\n\n**Map Compatibility:**\n- When opening a pinned map via `OpenOrCreate()`, map attributes are checked\n- If incompatible (type, key/value size, capacity differs), the old map is deleted and recreated\n- Incompatibility causes loss of previous map contents\n\n## Key/Value Interfaces\n\n### MapKey Interface\n\nAll map keys must implement the `MapKey` interface.\n\n```go\ntype MapKey interface {\n    fmt.Stringer\n    // New must return a pointer to a new MapKey of the same type.\n    New() MapKey\n}\n```\n\n**Requirements:**\n- Must be a pointer type (e.g., `*MyKey`)\n- Must implement `String()` for string representation\n- Must implement `New()` to create new zero-initialized instances\n- Size must be deterministic (used for MapSpec)\n\n**Example:**\n```go\ntype EndpointKey struct {\n    IP        types.IPv6\n    Family    uint8\n    Key       uint8\n    ClusterID uint16\n}\n\nfunc (k *EndpointKey) String() string {\n    // Return string representation\n}\n\nfunc (k *EndpointKey) New() MapKey {\n    return &EndpointKey{}\n}\n```\n\n### MapValue Interface\n\nAll map values must implement the `MapValue` interface.\n\n```go\ntype MapValue interface {\n    fmt.Stringer\n    // New must return a pointer to a new MapValue of the same type.\n    New() MapValue\n}\n```\n\n**Requirements:**\n- Must be a pointer type (e.g., `*MyValue`)\n- Must implement `String()` for string representation\n- Must implement `New()` to create new zero-initialized instances\n- Size must be deterministic (used for MapSpec)\n\n**Example:**\n```go\ntype EndpointValue struct {\n    IfIndex uint32\n    Unused  uint32\n}\n\nfunc (v *EndpointValue) String() string {\n    return fmt.Sprintf(\"ifindex=%d\", v.IfIndex)\n}\n\nfunc (v *EndpointValue) New() MapValue {\n    return &EndpointValue{}\n}\n```\n\n### MapPerCPUValue Interface\n\nFor per-CPU maps, values must implement `MapPerCPUValue`.\n\n```go\ntype MapPerCPUValue interface {\n    MapValue\n    // NewSlice returns a pointer to a slice of structs implementing MapValue.\n    NewSlice() any\n}\n```\n\n**Requirements:**\n- Must also implement `MapValue`\n- Must implement `NewSlice()` returning a pointer to a slice of values\n- Slice contains one element per CPU on the system\n\n**Example:**\n```go\ntype PerCPUStats struct {\n    Packets uint64\n    Bytes   uint64\n}\n\nfunc (s *PerCPUStats) NewSlice() any {\n    return &[]PerCPUStats{}\n}\n```\n\n### Concrete Example: EndpointKey\n\nThe `EndpointKey` type demonstrates the required implementation:\n\n```go\ntype EndpointKey struct {\n    IP        types.IPv6  // IPv6 address (IPv4 in lower 4 bytes)\n    Family    uint8       // EndpointKeyIPv4 (1) or EndpointKeyIPv6 (2)\n    Key       uint8       // Additional key field\n    ClusterID uint16      // Cluster identifier\n}\n\n// String returns \"IP:Key\" representation (e.g., \"10.0.0.1:0\")\nfunc (k EndpointKey) String() string { ... }\n\n// New returns a pointer to a new zero-initialized EndpointKey\nfunc (k EndpointKey) New() MapKey { ... }\n\n// NewEndpointKey convenience constructor\nfunc NewEndpointKey(addr netip.Addr, clusterID uint16) EndpointKey { ... }\n\n// ToAddr converts back to a network address\nfunc (k EndpointKey) ToAddr() netip.Addr { ... }\n```\n\n## Event System\n\nThe event system tracks map operations for auditing and debugging.\n\n### Action Type\n\nDescribes the type of map operation.\n\n```go\ntype Action uint8\n\nconst (\n    MapUpdate   Action = iota  // Key-value pair added/updated\n    MapDelete                  // Key deleted\n    MapDeleteAll               // All entries deleted at once\n)\n\nfunc (a Action) String() string  // \"update\", \"delete\", \"delete-all\"\n```\n\n### Event Type\n\nRepresents a single map operation event.\n\n```go\ntype Event struct {\n    Timestamp   time.Time\n    action      Action       // Use GetAction()\n    Key         MapKey       // The affected key\n    Value       MapValue     // The new value (nil for deletes)\n    DesiredAction DesiredAction\n    LastError   error\n}\n\n// Accessors\nfunc (e *Event) GetAction() string\nfunc (e Event) GetKey() string\nfunc (e Event) GetValue() string\nfunc (e Event) GetLastError() error\nfunc (e Event) GetDesiredAction() DesiredAction\n```\n\n### Event Subscription\n\n#### DumpAndSubscribe\n\nDumps existing buffered events and subscribes to future events.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) DumpAndSubscribe(\n    ctx context.Context,\n    callback EventCallbackFunc,\n    follow bool,\n)\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `ctx`: Context for event subscription lifetime\n- `callback`: Called for each event; if nil, only retrieves buffered events\n- `follow`: If true, continues observing new events; if false, only dumps existing\n\n**Type:**\n```go\ntype EventCallbackFunc func(Event)\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Dumping and subscription happen atomically (no events lost between operations)\n- If `callback` is nil, buffer is dumped but no subscription is created\n- If `follow` is false, buffer is dumped and subscription ends\n- If `follow` is true, subscription continues until context is canceled\n- Events are stored in a bounded ring buffer; old events are evicted when full\n\n**Example:**\n```go\nctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())\ndefer cancel()\n\nm.DumpAndSubscribe(ctx, func(e Event) {\n    log.Printf(\"[%s] %s -> %s\", e.GetAction(), e.GetKey(), e.GetValue())\n}, true)  // Follow new events\n\n// Process events until cancel() is called\n```\n\n#### IsEventsEnabled\n\nChecks if event buffering is enabled for the map.\n\n```go\nfunc (m *Map) IsEventsEnabled() bool\n```\n\n**Returns:** True if events are being recorded.\n\n## Collection Loading\n\n`LoadCollection` and `LoadAndAssign` load compiled eBPF ELF files into the kernel and manage the resulting maps and programs.\n\n### CollectionOptions\n\nConfiguration for collection loading.\n\n```go\ntype CollectionOptions struct {\n    ebpf.CollectionOptions\n\n    // Replacements for datapath runtime configs (DECLARE_CONFIG)\n    Constants any\n\n    // Maps to rename during loading\n    MapRenames []map[string]string\n\n    // Inner maps to replace\n    MapReplacements map[string]*Map\n\n    // Objects to keep during reachability pruning\n    Keep *set.Set[string]\n\n    // Path to dump constants to (for sysdumps)\n    ConfigDumpPath string\n}\n```\n\n### LoadCollection\n\nLoads an eBPF collection spec into the kernel.\n\n```go\nfunc LoadCollection(\n    logger *slog.Logger,\n    spec *ebpf.CollectionSpec,\n    opts *CollectionOptions,\n) (*ebpf.Collection, func() error, error)\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `logger`: For logging during load\n- `spec`: The eBPF collection specification\n- `opts`: Load options (can be nil for defaults)\n\n**Returns:**\n- `*ebpf.Collection`: The loaded collection\n- `func() error`: Commit function (must be called after programs are attached)\n- `error`: Load error\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Maps marked as pinned are automatically loaded from the pin path if they exist\n- Reachability analysis prunes unused maps and programs\n- Tail calls are resolved and populated into the calls map\n- Runtime constants (DECLARE_CONFIG) are applied to the spec\n- Maps can be renamed before loading\n- Returns a commit function that must be called after attaching all entrypoint programs\n- The commit function finalizes map pins for maps marked as needing replacement\n\n**Important:** The returned `commit()` function **must** be called after all entrypoint programs from the collection are attached to their kernel hooks. This ensures tail call maps are properly initialized before the kernel runs the programs.\n\n**Example:**\n```go\ncoll, commit, err := LoadCollection(logger, spec, opts)\nif err != nil {\n    return err\n}\ndefer coll.Close()\n\n// Attach programs to hooks\ncoll.Programs[\"ingress\"].Attach(...)\ncoll.Programs[\"egress\"].Attach(...)\n\n// Finalize pins\nif err := commit(); err != nil {\n    return err\n}\n```\n\n### LoadAndAssign\n\nLoads a collection and assigns the programs and maps to fields in a struct.\n\n```go\nfunc LoadAndAssign(\n    logger *slog.Logger,\n    to any,\n    spec *ebpf.CollectionSpec,\n    opts *CollectionOptions,\n) (func() error, error)\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `logger`: For logging\n- `to`: Pointer to struct with fields for programs and maps\n- `spec`: The collection spec\n- `opts`: Load options\n\n**Returns:**\n- `func() error`: Commit function (same as LoadCollection)\n- `error`: Load or assignment error\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Automatically analyzes the target struct to determine which objects to keep\n- Assigns programs and maps to matching exported fields by name\n- Unknown objects in the collection are pruned\n- Like `LoadCollection`, the returned commit function must be called after attaching programs\n\n**Example:**\n```go\ntype DatapathObjects struct {\n    IngresProgram   *ebpf.Program `ebpf:\"ingress\"`\n    EgressProgram   *ebpf.Program `ebpf:\"egress\"`\n    ConnectionsMap  *Map          `ebpf:\"connections\"`\n}\n\nobjs := &DatapathObjects{}\ncommit, err := LoadAndAssign(logger, objs, spec, opts)\nif err != nil {\n    return err\n}\n\n// Attach programs\nobjs.IngresProgram.Attach(...)\nobjs.EgressProgram.Attach(...)\n\n// Finalize\nreturn commit()\n```\n\n## Usage Examples\n\n### Basic Map Creation and CRUD\n\n```go\npackage main\n\nimport (\n    \"log\"\n    \"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/bpf\"\n    \"github.com/cilium/ebpf\"\n)\n\ntype MyKey struct {\n    ID uint32\n}\n\nfunc (k *MyKey) String() string {\n    return fmt.Sprintf(\"ID:%d\", k.ID)\n}\n\nfunc (k *MyKey) New() bpf.MapKey {\n    return &MyKey{}\n}\n\ntype MyValue struct {\n    Count uint64\n}\n\nfunc (v *MyValue) String() string {\n    return fmt.Sprintf(\"Count:%d\", v.Count)\n}\n\nfunc (v *MyValue) New() bpf.MapValue {\n    return &MyValue{}\n}\n\nfunc main() {\n    // Create map\n    m := bpf.NewMap(\"my_map\", ebpf.Hash, &MyKey{}, &MyValue{}, 10000, 0)\n\n    // Open or create the map\n    if err := m.OpenOrCreate(); err != nil {\n        log.Fatalf(\"Failed to create map: %v\", err)\n    }\n    defer m.Close()\n\n    // Insert\n    key := &MyKey{ID: 42}\n    value := &MyValue{Count: 100}\n    if err := m.Update(key, value); err != nil {\n        log.Fatalf(\"Update failed: %v\", err)\n    }\n\n    // Lookup\n    retrieved, err := m.Lookup(key)\n    if err != nil {\n        log.Fatalf(\"Lookup failed: %v\", err)\n    }\n    log.Printf(\"Retrieved: %v\", retrieved)\n\n    // Delete\n    if err := m.Delete(key); err != nil {\n        log.Fatalf(\"Delete failed: %v\", err)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Iteration with DumpWithCallback\n\n```go\nfunc dumpMap(m *bpf.Map) error {\n    return m.DumpWithCallback(func(key bpf.MapKey, value bpf.MapValue) {\n        log.Printf(\"  %s -> %s\", key.String(), value.String())\n    })\n}\n```\n\n### Reliable Iteration with Recovery\n\n```go\nfunc reliableIterateMap(m *bpf.Map) error {\n    stats := bpf.NewDumpStats(m)\n\n    err := m.DumpReliablyWithCallback(func(key bpf.MapKey, value bpf.MapValue) {\n        log.Printf(\"  %s -> %s\", key.String(), value.String())\n    }, stats)\n\n    if err != nil && err != bpf.ErrMaxLookup {\n        return err\n    }\n\n    log.Printf(\"Iteration stats: lookups=%d, failures=%d, completed=%v, duration=%v\",\n        stats.Lookup, stats.LookupFailed, stats.Completed, stats.Duration())\n\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\n### Batch Iterator\n\n```go\nfunc iterateWithBatch(ctx context.Context, m *bpf.Map) error {\n    iter := bpf.NewBatchIterator[MyKey, MyValue](m)\n\n    count := 0\n    for key, value := range iter.IterateAll(ctx) {\n        log.Printf(\"  %s -> %s\", key.String(), value.String())\n        count++\n    }\n\n    if err := iter.Err(); err != nil {\n        log.Printf(\"Iteration error: %v\", err)\n        return err\n    }\n\n    log.Printf(\"Iterated %d entries\", count)\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\n### Event Subscription\n\n```go\nfunc subscribeToEvents(ctx context.Context, m *bpf.Map) {\n    m.DumpAndSubscribe(ctx, func(event bpf.Event) {\n        log.Printf(\"[%s] %s -> %s (error: %v)\",\n            event.GetAction(),\n            event.GetKey(),\n            event.GetValue(),\n            event.GetLastError())\n    }, true)  // follow future events\n\n    // Listen for events until context is canceled\n}\n```\n\n### Pinning and Unpinning\n\n```go\nfunc manageMapPins() error {\n    m := bpf.NewMap(\"shared_map\", ebpf.Hash, &MyKey{}, &MyValue{}, 10000, 0)\n\n    // Create and pin\n    if err := m.OpenOrCreate(); err != nil {\n        return err\n    }\n    defer m.Close()\n\n    // Map is now pinned to the filesystem at <CiliumPath>/shared_map\n    path, _ := m.Path()\n    log.Printf(\"Map pinned to: %s\", path)\n\n    // Later, in another process, open the pinned map\n    m2, err := bpf.OpenMap(path, &MyKey{}, &MyValue{})\n    if err != nil {\n        return err\n    }\n    defer m2.Close()\n\n    // Unpin the map from the filesystem\n    if err := m2.Unpin(); err != nil {\n        return err\n    }\n\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\n### Collection Loading\n\n```go\nfunc loadDatapath(logger *slog.Logger) error {\n    // Load ELF file and parse spec\n    spec, err := ebpf.LoadCollectionSpec(\"bpf_program.o\")\n    if err != nil {\n        return err\n    }\n\n    opts := &bpf.CollectionOptions{\n        CollectionOptions: ebpf.CollectionOptions{\n            Programs: ebpf.ProgramOptions{\n                KernelTypes: btfSpec,\n            },\n            Maps: ebpf.MapOptions{\n                PinPath: bpf.CiliumPath(),\n            },\n        },\n    }\n\n    coll, commit, err := bpf.LoadCollection(logger, spec, opts)\n    if err != nil {\n        return err\n    }\n    defer coll.Close()\n\n    // Attach programs\n    if err := attachPrograms(coll); err != nil {\n        return err\n    }\n\n    // Finalize map pins\n    if err := commit(); err != nil {\n        return err\n    }\n\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\n### Deletion During Iteration\n\n```go\nfunc filterMap(m *bpf.Map, shouldDelete func(bpf.MapKey) bool) error {\n    stats := bpf.NewDumpStats(m)\n\n    return m.DumpReliablyWithCallback(func(key bpf.MapKey, value bpf.MapValue) {\n        if shouldDelete(key) {\n            // Safe to delete within the callback\n            if err := m.DeleteLocked(key); err != nil {\n                log.Printf(\"Delete failed: %v\", err)\n            }\n        }\n    }, stats)\n}\n```\n\n### Map with Cache and Events\n\n```go\nfunc setupMapWithTracking(logger *slog.Logger) (*bpf.Map, error) {\n    m := bpf.NewMap(\"tracked_map\", ebpf.Hash, &MyKey{}, &MyValue{}, 10000, 0).\n        WithCache().\n        WithEvents(option.BPFEventBufferConfig{\n            Enabled: true,\n            MaxSize: 1000,\n            TTL:     5 * time.Minute,\n        })\n\n    if err := m.OpenOrCreate(); err != nil {\n        return nil, err\n    }\n\n    // Subscribe to events\n    ctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())\n    go func() {\n        defer cancel()\n        m.DumpAndSubscribe(ctx, func(event bpf.Event) {\n            log.Printf(\"Event: %s\", event.GetAction())\n        }, true)\n    }()\n\n    return m, nil\n}\n```\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### Common Errors\n\n- **ErrMapNotOpened**: Returned when operations are attempted on a map that hasn't been opened\n- **ErrKeyNotExist**: Returned from Lookup when key doesn't exist (wrapped in ebpf errors)\n- **ErrMaxLookup**: Returned from DumpReliablyWithCallback when iteration limit exceeded\n- **ErrMapIncompatible**: Returned when LoadCollection encounters incompatible pinned maps\n\n### Synchronization and Error Recovery\n\nWhen a map has caching enabled via `WithCache()`, failed Update or Delete operations are tracked:\n\n1. The error is recorded in the cache entry\n2. An error resolver controller is scheduled\n3. The controller periodically retries failed operations\n4. Once resolved, the cache entry is updated to reflect the successful operation\n\nThis provides resilience against transient failures.\n\n## Design Patterns and Best Practices\n\n### Pattern: Stateful Map Operations with Caching\n\nUse `WithCache()` when you need to track synchronization state or ensure reliable operation delivery:\n\n```go\nm := bpf.NewMap(name, mapType, key, value, maxEntries, flags).\n    WithCache().\n    WithGroupName(\"my_maps\")\n\nm.OpenOrCreate()\n// Updates are tracked and retried on failure\n```\n\n### Pattern: Pinning Maps for Persistence\n\nMaps are pinned by default via `OpenOrCreate()`. To prevent pinning (for temporary maps), use `CreateUnpinned()`:\n\n```go\n// Persistent map (default)\nm := bpf.NewMap(name, ...)\nm.OpenOrCreate()  // Pinned at <CiliumPath>/name\n\n// Temporary map\nm2 := bpf.NewMap(name, ...)\nm2.CreateUnpinned()  // Not persisted, destroyed on process exit\n```\n\n### Pattern: Safe Concurrent Dumping with Deletion\n\nWhen dumping a map where entries may be modified concurrently, use `DumpReliablyWithCallback()` with `DeleteLocked()`:\n\n```go\nstats := bpf.NewDumpStats(m)\nm.DumpReliablyWithCallback(func(key bpf.MapKey, value bpf.MapValue) {\n    if isExpired(value) {\n        m.DeleteLocked(key)  // Safe here - holds lock\n    }\n}, stats)\n```\n\n### Pattern: Batch Processing Large Maps\n\nFor efficient iteration of very large maps, prefer `BatchIterator` over `DumpWithCallback`:\n\n```go\n// Efficient batch processing\niter := bpf.NewBatchIterator[K, V](m,\n    bpf.WithStartingChunkSize(4096))\n\nfor k, v := range iter.IterateAll(ctx) {\n    processEntry(k, v)\n}\n```\n\n### Pattern: Map Lifecycle in Agents\n\n1. Create and configure maps before datapath loading\n2. Call `OpenOrCreate()` on all maps\n3. Load eBPF collection after maps exist\n4. Call `commit()` after attaching programs\n5. Subscribe to events if needed\n6. Close maps on shutdown\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
